 <body>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:right;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Exhibit 99.1</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><img src="img247042425_0.jpg" alt="img247042425_0.jpg" style="width:174px;height:86px;">&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:14.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Athira Pharma Reports Third Quarter 2022 Financial Results and Recent Clinical and Corporate Updates</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Independent, unblinded, interim efficacy and futility analysis of Phase 2/3 LIFT-AD study in mild-to-moderate Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease patients supports potential clinically meaningful activity of fosgonimeton without background acetylcholinesterase therapy and mitigates program risk</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:center;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Strong balance sheet to support clinical development pipeline through key data inflection points</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">BOTHELL, Wash., Nov. 10, 2022</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> &#x2014; </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Athira Pharma, Inc.</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> (NASDAQ: ATHA), a late clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on developing small molecules to restore neuronal health and slow neurodegeneration, today announced the company&#x2019;s financial results for the third quarter ended September 30, 2022 and reviewed recent clinical and corporate updates.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#x201c;During the third quarter, we undertook a systematic and data-driven process to determine the next steps for our Phase 2/3 LIFT-AD study of fosgonimeton in mild-to-moderate Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease (AD) patients.  Most recently, we were encouraged to report that an independent, unblinded, interim efficacy and futility analysis supported the potential clinically meaningful activity of fosgonimeton without background therapy (acetylcholinesterase inhibitors) and determined that, with the additional enrollment of fewer than 150 patients, the study will be well powered for the primary endpoint given the preliminary effect size observed,&#x201d; stated Mark Litton, Ph.D., President and Chief Executive Officer of Athira.</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:justify;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#x201c;The exploratory Phase 2 ACT-AD study in the same patient population suggested benefits in measurements of cognition, function and neuroprotection, and the results of the LIFT-AD interim analysis corroborate those findings in approximately 100 patients not on background therapy. We now look forward to completing enrollment of the Phase 2/3 LIFT-AD study in mid-2023 and to reporting topline data in early 2024. Importantly, we are pleased to have a strong balance sheet that can support our programs through a number of key data inflection points and beyond,&#x201d; concluded Dr. Litton.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Clinical Update:</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Fosgonimeton (ATH-1017)</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> is a small molecule specifically designed to enhance the activity of Hepatocyte Growth Factor (HGF) and its receptor, MET.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:3.333%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">LIFT-AD Phase 2/3 study in mild-to-moderate Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease (</font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">NCT04488419</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">)</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Following results from the exploratory ACT-AD trial, Athira proactively amended the entry criteria for the LIFT-AD trial in September 2022 to investigate the effects of fosgonimeton compared with placebo, without background therapy. In October 2022, following an unblinded interim efficacy and futility analysis, an independent data monitoring committee recommended continuation of the LIFT-AD study of fosgonimeton in patients with mild-to-moderate AD. The committee also determined that, with the additional enrollment of fewer than 150 patients for a </font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <hr style="page-break-after:always;">
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;visibility:hidden;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;"></font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">total enrollment of less than 300 patients without background therapy, the study will be well powered for the primary endpoint given the preliminary effect size observed.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:3.333%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">ACT-AD Phase 2 study in mild-to-moderate Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease (</font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">NCT04491006</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">)*</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Additional data from the ACT-AD Phase 2 study were presented in August 2022 at the Alzheimer's Association International Conference 2022 (AAIC). This included a numerical, but not statistically significant, improvement in the secondary endpoint ADCS-ADL23, a functional measure of independence, and a statistically significant improvement in plasma levels of neurofilament light chain (NfL), a validated fluid biomarker of neurodegeneration, in a prespecified subgroup of subjects treated with fosgonimeton without background therapy compared with placebo at 26 weeks.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:3.333%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Open Label Extension (OLEX) study (</font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">NCT04886063</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">)</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The Open Label Extension (OLEX) study for the ACT-AD and LIFT-AD studies continues, with over 200 patients currently enrolled. As of October 2022, more than 90 percent of patients who have completed either study have elected to participate in the OLEX study. </font></div></div>
  <p style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">SHAPE Phase 2 study in Parkinson&#x2019;s disease dementia or Dementia with Lewy bodies (</font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">NCT04831281</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">)</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The SHAPE Phase 2 proof-of-concept study of fosgonimeton in participants with Parkinson&#x2019;s disease dementia or Dementia with Lewy bodies is approximately 40% enrolled.  </font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">The company is evaluating next steps for this program in light of the ACT-AD results and the interim LIFT-AD analysis.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">ATH-1020 </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">is an orally available, brain-penetrant small molecule designed to enhance the HGF/MET system that is being advanced as a potential treatment candidate for neuropsychiatric indications.</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:3.333%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Phase 1 study of ATH-1020 in healthy volunteers (</font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">NCT05169671</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">)</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Athira is conducting a Phase 1 study to evaluate the safety, tolerability, and pharmacokinetics of ATH-1020 in approximately 68 healthy young and elderly volunteers. The single ascending dose escalation portion of the trial has been completed with no safety findings.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Research and Development Update:</font></p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Preclinical data presented at </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Alzheimer's Association International Conference (AAIC) 2022</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Preclinical data presented at the AAIC conference in August 2022 demonstrated that fosgo-AM, the active metabolite of fosgonimeton, can promote neurotrophic effects and offer protection against neurological insults central to neurodegeneration in animal models of Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease. Additional data presented highlighted the ability of new orally available small molecule positive modulators of HGF/MET to reverse memory deficits in preclinical models. </font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;font-style:italic;min-width:fit-content;">Upcoming data presentations at scientific meetings</font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:8.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">At the Society for Neuroscience 2022 Annual Meeting (November 12-16, 2022; San Diego), Athira will present data highlighting the effects of fosgonimeton in preclinical models of Parkinson&#x2019;s disease as well as preclinical data on small molecule positive modulators of HGF/MET in diabetic neuropathic pain.</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>

  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:8.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">At the 15</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">th</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> Clinical Trials on Alzheimer&#x2019;s Disease (CTAD) Annual Meeting (November 29-December 2, 2022; San Francisco), Athira will give a poster presentation on fosgonimeton&#x2019;s effect on additional plasma biomarkers from the ACT-AD study and their relevance to clinical endpoints.</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.2410416666666666;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:8.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">At the 33</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;vertical-align:super;font-size:7.37pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">rd</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> International Symposium on Amyotrophic</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Lateral Sclerosis and Motor Neuron Disease (December 6-9, 2022; virtual), Athira will present preclinical data demonstrating neuroprotective effects of ATH-1105, a small molecule positive modulator of HGF/MET, in an animal model of Amyotrophic Lateral Sclerosis (ALS).</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"><br></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Arial&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.3225;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Financial Results</font><font style="color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:12.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> </font></p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Cash Position</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">. Cash, cash equivalents and investments were $260.0 million as of September 30, 2022, compared with $319.7 million as of December 31, 2021. Cash used in operations was $56.8 million for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, compared with $24.9 million for the nine months ended September 30, 2021.<br></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Research and Development (R&amp;D) Expenses</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">. R&amp;D expenses were $17.0 million for the quarter ended September 30, 2022, compared with $10.7 million for the same period in 2021. The increase was driven primarily by costs related to increased clinical trial activities, expanded personnel, and increased preclinical research and development expenses.  <br></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">&#160;</font></div></div>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">General and Administrative (G&amp;A) Expenses. </font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">G&amp;A expenses were $7.2 million for the quarter ended September 30, 2022, compared with $7.1 million for same period in 2021.</font></div></div>
  <p style="margin-left:6.667%;text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="white-space:pre-wrap;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"></font>&#160;</p>
  <div style="margin-left:3.333%;text-indent:0.0%;display:flex;margin-top:0.0pt;line-height:1.15;justify-content:flex-start;align-items:baseline;margin-bottom:0.0pt;min-width:3.333%;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:10.0pt;font-family:&quot;Times New Roman&quot;, serif;min-width:fit-content;text-indent:0;display:inline-flex;font-family:Times New Roman;justify-content:flex-start;min-width:3.447919145106397%;">&#x2022;</font><div style="display:inline;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Net Loss</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">. The company reported a net loss of $20.2 million, or $0.53 per share, for the quarter ended September 30, 2022, compared with a net loss of $15.7 million, or $0.42 per share, for the same period in 2021. </font></div></div>
  <p style="text-indent:0.0%;font-size:10.0pt;margin-top:13.5pt;line-height:1.15;font-family:Times New Roman;margin-bottom:0.0pt;text-align:left;"><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:bold;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">About Athira Pharma, Inc.</font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"><br>Athira Pharma, Inc., headquartered in the Seattle, Washington area, is a late clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on developing small molecules to restore neuronal health and slow neurodegeneration. Athira aims to provide rapid cognitive improvement and alter the course of neurological diseases with its novel mechanism of action. Athira is currently advancing its pipeline of therapeutic candidates targeting the HGF/MET neurotrophic system for Alzheimer&#x2019;s disease, Parkinson&#x2019;s disease dementia, Dementia with Lewy bodies, and neuropsychiatric indications. For more information, visit </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">www.athira.com</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">. You can also follow Athira on </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Facebook</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">, </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">LinkedIn</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> and @athirapharma on </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Twitter</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;"> and </font><font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">Instagram</font></font><font style="background-color:rgba(0,0,0,0);color:rgba(0,0,0,1);white-space:pre-wrap;font-weight:normal;font-size:11.0pt;font-family:&quot;Calibri&quot;, sans-serif;min-width:fit-content;">.</font></p>
